# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

implemented across multiple Java source files in the storage module. The core LogSegment class (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogSegment.java) represents a single log segment file and manages the actual log data through FileRecords (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/record/FileRecords.java) along with index files. Each LogSegment contains three types of indexes: OffsetIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/OffsetIndex.java) for mapping offsets to file positions, TimeIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/TimeIndex.java) for timestamp-based lookups, and TransactionIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/TransactionIndex.java) for tracking aborted transactions. These index classes extend AbstractIndex (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/AbstractIndex.java), which provides common memory-mapped file operations. The LazyIndex class (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LazyIndex.java) provides lazy loading of indexes to optimize memory usage. LogConfig (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogConfig.java) manages all log configuration parameters including retention policies, index settings, and cleanup policies. LogFileUtils (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogFileUtils.java) provides utility methods for file naming and offset extraction from filenames. LocalLog (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LocalLog.java) manages collections of segments within a partition directory and handles segment lifecycle (creation, rolling, deletion). UnifiedLog (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/UnifiedLog.java) is the main abstraction representing the complete log for a partition, coordinating LocalLog with producer state management. LogLoader (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogLoader.java) handles log recovery on startup from checkpoint files, loading segments and recovering indexes if corrupted. ProducerStateManager (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/ProducerStateManager.java) manages producer state snapshots for transaction support. Checkpoint files are managed through OffsetCheckpointFile (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/OffsetCheckpointFile.java) which stores recovery points and log start offsets, and LeaderEpochCheckpointFile (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/LeaderEpochCheckpointFile.java) which stores leader epoch information for log truncation decisions. The LeaderEpochFileCache (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/epoch/LeaderEpochFileCache.java) caches the leader epoch checkpoint for quick lookups during replication. Log cleaning is handled by Cleaner (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/Cleaner.java) and LogCleaner (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogCleaner.java), which implement log compaction for compacted topics with configuration via CleanerConfig (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/CleanerConfig.java). For tiered storage support, RemoteLogManager (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/log/remote/storage/RemoteLogManager.java) coordinates offloading segments to remote storage, while RemoteIndexCache (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/RemoteIndexCache.java) caches indexes for remotely stored segments and RemoteLogManagerConfig (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/log/remote/storage/RemoteLogManagerConfig.java) manages tiered storage configuration. The initialization flow starts with LogLoader.load() during broker startup, which reads checkpoint files to determine recovery points, then reconstructs segment and index files. LogSegment.open() creates segment instances from on-disk files, recovering indexes if necessary. The LazyIndex wrapper ensures indexes are only loaded when accessed. This architecture ensures durability through checkpoint files persisted at configurable intervals, enables efficient log recovery from unclean shutdowns, supports multiple index types for diverse query patterns, and provides pluggable tiered storage for cost-effective retention of large logs.\"\n}\n",
